***слыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слыть.html>слыть</a> (14196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slyti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱlew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλύω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klúō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I hear, listen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλυτός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klutós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">famous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">inclūtus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">renowned</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слыть.html>слыть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прослыть.html>прослы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pass (for), to have the reputation (for), to be said / reputed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчего.html>отчего́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прослыть.html>прослы́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарлатан.html>шарлата́ном</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отчего.html>отчего́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прослыть.html>прослы́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скандалист.html>скандали́стом</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otčevó <b>proslýl</b> ja šarlatánom, otčevó <b>proslýl</b> ja skandalístom?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why did I get the reputation of a charlatan, why am I known as a scandalist? (<b>Sergey Yesenin</b>, «<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обманывать.html>обма́нывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́ну</a>...»)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***слыхать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ть</a> (2834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slyxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hear of, to hear from</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Note that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ть</a></b> has a limited usage, and in standard language it not conjugated in the present tense, future tense or imperative. It is used only as the infinitive or in the past tense:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">O njóm ničevó ne <b>slyxátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">One <b>hears</b> nothing from him.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давно.html>давно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ть</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">O nej davnó ničevó ne <b>slyxátʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She hasn’t been <b>heard</b> from in a long time.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Slyxáli</b> li vy ob étom?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Have you <b>heard</b> about it?</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>Нет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́л</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Net, ne <b>slyxál</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">No, I haven’t heard.</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slýšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слыхивать.html>слы́хивать</a> (18190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slyxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхивать.html>слы́хивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slýxivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to hear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слыхать.html>слыха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slyxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>, <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slýšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.</li></ul>

***слышать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a> (267)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slỳšati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱlew-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slýšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:услышать.html>услы́шать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smell, to feel (a smell)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шу</a></b> како́й-то <a href = vnd.unilang:странный.html>стра́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>за́пах</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>slýšu</b> kakój-to stránnyj zápax.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I smell something strange./I feel some strange smell.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слышаться.html>слы́шаться</a> (2623)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slýšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышаться.html>слы́шаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slýšatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послышаться.html>послы́шаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be heard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слышаться.html>слы́шалось</a></b> чьё-то <a href = vnd.unilang:пение.html>пе́ние</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vdalí <b>slýšalosʹ</b> čʹjó-to pénije.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In the distance singing was heard</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be felt, to be smelled</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slýšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a> (1756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышный.html>слы́шный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slýšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slýšno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>audibly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slýšno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>it is audible, one can hear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne otsjúda vsjó óčenʹ xorošó <b>slýšno</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I can hear everything very well from here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>it is known, there is information <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in questions or negative constructions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što o njóm <b>slýšno</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What is known about him?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>Про</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давно.html>давно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pro nevó davnó ničevó ne <b>slýšno</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There has been no information about him for a long time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слюна.html>слюна́</a> (5064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slina</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слюна.html>слюна́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sljuná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слюна.html>слюны́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слюни.html>слю́ни</a> (14546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slina</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*H₂leyH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">слина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:слюна.html>слю́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sljúna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">slina</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">ślina</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слюни.html>слю́ни</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sljúni</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слюни.html>слюне́й</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слюнка.html>слю́нки</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> saliva, drool</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slękъtь</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слякоть.html>сля́коть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sljákotʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слякоть.html>сля́коти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слякоть.html>сля́коти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слякоть.html>сля́котей</a></b>)

***смазать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смазать.html>сма́зать</a> (8269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смазать.html>сма́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smázatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смазывать.html>сма́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smear, to grease, to oil, to lubricate, to dub
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смазать.html>сма́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:йод.html>йо́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smázatʹ</b> jódom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to paint with iodine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to smear, to wipe off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grease someone's palm</li>
<li><i>(a question, a problem)</i> to slur
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смазать.html>сма́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smázatʹ</b> voprós</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slur over a question</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(photography)</i> to blur</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bash, to dot</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смазка.html>сма́зка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smázka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***смазывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смазывать.html>сма́зывать</a> (11788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смазать.html>сма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смазывать.html>сма́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смазать.html>сма́зать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smear, to grease, to oil, to lubricate, to dub
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смазывать.html>сма́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:йод.html>йо́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smázyvatʹ</b> jódom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to paint with iodine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to smear, to wipe off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grease someone's palm</li>
<li><i>(a question, a problem)</i> to slur
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смазывать.html>сма́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smázyvatʹ</b> voprós</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slur over a question</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(photography)</i> to blur</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смак.html>смак</a> (25836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">smak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">taste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">gismac</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">taste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">gesmac(h)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">taste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Geschmack</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">taste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смак.html>смак</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smak</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смак.html>сма́ка</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смаковать.html>смаку́емый</a> (19087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
